 <tr style="mso-yfti-irow:2">
  <td width="270" valign="top" style="width:134.9pt;border:solid windowtext 1.0pt;

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">（保留，送院會二讀前黨團協商）</span></p>
  </td>
  <td width="270" valign="top" style="width:134.9pt;border-top:none;border-left:
  none;border-bottom:solid windowtext 1.0pt;border-right:solid windowtext 1.0pt;
  mso-border-top-alt:solid windowtext .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid windowtext .5pt;
  mso-border-alt:solid windowtext .5pt;padding:1.4pt 1.4pt 1.4pt 1.4pt">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
  </td>
  <td width="270" valign="top" style="width:134.95pt;border-top:none;border-left:
  none;border-bottom:solid windowtext 1.0pt;border-right:solid windowtext 1.0pt;
  mso-border-top-alt:solid windowtext .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid windowtext .5pt;
  mso-border-alt:solid windowtext .5pt;padding:1.4pt 1.4pt 1.4pt 1.4pt">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康中黑體">民進黨黨團提案：</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第二條之一　（食品安全會報之組成）</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">為管理食品衛生安全及品質，行政院應設食品安全會報，由行政院長擔任召集人，召集相關部會首長、專家學者及民間團體代表共同組成，職司跨部會協調食品安全風險管理措施，建立食品衛生安全之預警及稽核制度，至少每三個月開會一次。召集人應指定一名政務委員擔任食品安全會報執行長，並設食品安全專案辦公室，統籌相關事務運作。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">前項食品安全會報所決議之工作目標，各相關部會應落實執行，行政院應每季追蹤管考並公布之，並應送立法院備查。食品安全會報召集人應將每年工作成果向立法院報告。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康中黑體">委員劉建國等<span lang="EN-US">22</span>人提案：</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第二條之一　行政院為維護國人享有健康安全食品並確實保障國人健康等基本政策與監督其實施，設食品安全委員會。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">食品安全委員會以行政院副院長為主任委員，有關部會首長、全國性食品安全團體代表、全國性企業經營者代表及學者、專家為委員。其組織規程由行政院定之。</span></p>
  </td>
  <td width="270" valign="top" style="width:134.95pt;border-top:none;border-left:
  none;border-bottom:solid windowtext 1.0pt;border-right:solid windowtext 1.0pt;
  mso-border-top-alt:solid windowtext .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid windowtext .5pt;
  mso-border-alt:solid windowtext .5pt;padding:1.4pt 1.4pt 1.4pt 1.4pt">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
  </td>
  <td width="270" valign="top" style="width:134.95pt;border-top:none;border-left:
  none;border-bottom:solid windowtext 1.0pt;border-right:solid windowtext 1.0pt;
  mso-border-top-alt:solid windowtext .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid windowtext .5pt;
  mso-border-alt:solid windowtext .5pt;padding:1.4pt 1.4pt 1.4pt 1.4pt">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康中黑體">民進黨黨團提案：</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、本條新增。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">二、此次餿水油事件，赫然發現廢食用油竟是三不管地帶，</span><span lang="EN-US">2009</span><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:
  &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">年監察院調查大型速食業者炸油使用情形時，調查報告中寫明「環保署對於廢食用油之管理，未盡周全及確實，應予檢討改進」，顯然「行政院食品安全會報」在做為跨部會溝通平台或食品衛生安全的預警制度之機制上，未能發揮應有之功能。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">三、現行食品安全會報屬於任務編組，等到食安問題發生才開會因應，淪為應變會報，無法常態性處理食品安全各項跨部會整合問題。爰新增本條文，行政院應將食品安全會報由半年開會一次改為至少每三個月開會一次，除由行政院長擔任召集人外，並由一名政務委員擔任執行長，設置食品安全專案辦公室，聘請專業人員，橫向整合管理各部會與食安相關業務，通盤解決由生產端至消費端的風險管理，定期追蹤，具體落實食品安全管理措施。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">四、為避免相關部會未能具體落實食安會報決議之工作目標，要求行政院應每季追蹤管考並公布之，召集人應每年將工作成果向立法院報告。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康中黑體">委員劉建國等<span lang="EN-US">22</span>人提案：</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、本條新增。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">二、綜觀我國食品安全管理係採分段管理的分工模式，涉及部會包括衛生署、農委會、環保署、經濟部、財政部、教育部及行政院消保處……等。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">三、鑑於食品安全管理之複雜性，世界各國均非由單一機關獨立完成，而是由不同機關分工，以避免各機關間各行其事，主要先進國家均更進而成立具有實體機關性質之跨部會協調監管單位（或機構），以執行綜合監督、組織協調及處理重大事件等任務。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">四、行政院應協調各部會共同組成「食品安全委員會」，以建立政府監管部門之專責指揮中心，負責各部門間之協調統合，提升效率。「食品安全委員會」之建置應比照前「行政院消費者保護委員會」，召集人或主任委員應由行政院副院長兼任。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康中黑體">委員田秋堇等<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人所提修正動議：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第二條之一　為管理食品衛生安全及品質，行政院應設食品安全會報，由行政院長擔任召集人，召集相關部會首長、專家學者及民間團體代表共同組成，職司跨部會協調食品安全風險管理措施，建立食品衛生安全之預警及稽核制度，至少每三個月開會一次。召集人應指定一名政務委員擔任食品安全會報執行長，其幕僚作業由衛生福利部兼辦。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">前項食品安全會報所決議之工作目標，各相關部會應落實執行，行政院應每季追蹤管考並公布之，並應送立法院備查。食品安全會報召集人應將每年工作成果向立法院報告。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康中黑體">委員江惠貞等<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人所提修正動議：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第二條之一　為加強全國食品安全事務之協調、監督、推動與查緝，行政院設置食品安全衛生會報，由行政院長擔任召集人，召集相關部會首長、專家學者及民間團體代表共同組成，職司跨部會協調食品安全風險管理措施，建立食品安全衛生之預警及稽核制度，至少每三個月舉行會議一次。召集人應指定一名政務委員擔任食品安全會報執行長，並設食品安全專案辦公室，統籌相關事務運作。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">各直轄市、縣（市）應設置食品安全衛生會報，職司跨局處協調食品安全衛生管理措施，至少每三個月舉行會議一次。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">前項之食品安全衛生會報之組織、會議等設置規定，由衛生福利部定之。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康中黑體">審查會：</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第二條之一條文：民進黨黨團、委員劉建國等</span><span lang="EN-US">22</span><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:
  &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">人提案及委員田秋堇等</span><span lang="EN-US">4</span><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">人、委員江惠貞等</span><span lang="EN-US">4</span><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">人所提修正動議均保留。</span></p>
  </td>

  <td width="270" valign="top" style="width:134.9pt;border:solid windowtext 1.0pt;
  border-top:none;mso-border-top-alt:solid windowtext .5pt;mso-border-alt:solid windowtext .5pt;
  padding:1.4pt 1.4pt 1.4pt 1.4pt">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">（保留，送院會二讀前黨團協商）</span></p>
  </td>
  <td width="270" valign="top" style="width:134.9pt;border-top:none;border-left:
  none;border-bottom:solid windowtext 1.0pt;border-right:solid windowtext 1.0pt;
  mso-border-top-alt:solid windowtext .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid windowtext .5pt;
  mso-border-alt:solid windowtext .5pt;padding:1.4pt 1.4pt 1.4pt 1.4pt">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
  </td>
  <td width="270" valign="top" style="width:134.95pt;border-top:none;border-left:
  none;border-bottom:solid windowtext 1.0pt;border-right:solid windowtext 1.0pt;
  mso-border-top-alt:solid windowtext .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid windowtext .5pt;
  mso-border-alt:solid windowtext .5pt;padding:1.4pt 1.4pt 1.4pt 1.4pt">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康中黑體">委員田秋堇等<span lang="EN-US">26</span>人提案：</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第三條　本法用詞，定義如下：</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、食品：指供人飲食、咀嚼<u>或以其他方式攝入體內之可食用物質，但嗜好性之菸、酒及檳榔除外。</u></span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">二、特殊營養食品：指嬰兒與較大嬰兒配方食品、特定疾病配方食品及其他經中央主管機關許可得供特殊營養需求者使用之配方食品。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">三、食品添加物：指為食品著色、調味、防腐、漂白、乳化、增加香味、安定品質、促進發酵、增加稠度、強化營養、防止氧化或其他必要目的，加入、接觸於食品之單方或複方物質。複方食品添加物使用之添加物僅限由中央主管機關准用之食品添加物組成，前述准用之單方食品添加物皆應有中央主管機關之<u>審核</u>准用許可證字號。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">四、食品器具：指與食品或食品添加物直接接觸之器械、工具或器皿。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">五、食品容器或包裝：指與食品或食品添加物直接接觸之容器或包裹物。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">六、食品用洗潔劑：指用於消毒或洗滌食品、食品器具、食品容器或包裝之物質。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">七、食品業者：指從事食品或食品添加物之製造、加工、調配、包裝、運送、貯存、販賣、輸入、輸出或從事食品器具、食品容器或包裝、食品用洗潔劑之製造、加工、輸入、輸出或販賣之業者。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">八、標示：指於食品、食品添加物、食品用洗潔劑、食品器具、食品容器或包裝上，記載品名或為說明之文字、圖畫、記號或附加之說明書。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">九、營養標示：指於食品容器或包裝上，記載食品之營養成分、含量及營養宣稱。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">十、查驗：指查核及檢驗。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">十一、基因改造：指使用基因工程或分子生物技術，將遺傳物質轉移或轉殖入活細胞或生物體，產生基因重組現象，使表現具外源基因特性或使自身特定基因無法表現之相關技術。但不包括傳統育種、同科物種之細胞及原生質體融合、雜交、誘變、體外受精、體細胞變異及染色體倍增等技術。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康中黑體">委員劉建國等<span lang="EN-US">22</span>人提案：</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第三條　本法用詞，定義如下：</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、食品：指供人飲食或咀嚼之產品及其原料。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">二、特殊營養食品：指嬰兒與較大嬰兒配方食品、特定疾病配方食品及其他經中央主管機關許可得供特殊營養需求者使用之配方食品。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">三、食品添加物：指為食品著色、調味、防腐、漂白、乳化、增加香味、安定品質、促進發酵、增加稠度、強化營養、防止氧化或其他必要目的，加入、接觸於食品之單方或複方物質。複方食品添加物使用之添加物僅限由中央主管機關准用之食品添加物組成，前述准用之單方食品添加物皆應有中央主管機關之准用<u>許可證字號</u>。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">四、食品器具：指與食品或食品添加物直接接觸之器械、工具或器皿。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">五、食品容器或包裝：指與食品或食品添加物直接接觸之容器或包裹物。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">六、食品用洗潔劑：指用於消毒或洗滌食品、食品器具、食品容器或包裝之物質。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">七、食品業者：指從事食品或食品添加物之製造、加工、調配、包裝、運送、貯存、販賣、輸入、輸出或從事食品器具、食品容器或包裝、食品用洗潔劑之製造、加工、輸入、輸出或販賣之業者。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">八、標示：指於食品、食品添加物、食品用洗潔劑、食品器具、食品容器或包裝上，記載品名或為說明之文字、圖畫、記號或附加之說明書。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">九、營養標示：指於食品容器或包裝上，記載食品之營養成分、含量及營養宣稱。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">十、查驗：指查核及檢驗。</span></p>

  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:

  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、食品定義排除菸、酒及檳榔，並做部分修正，以使管灌飲食亦屬食品管理。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">二、本條第一項第三款所指中央主管機關之准用許可字號，係指行政機關許可證之字號，而非本法施行細則第三條所稱之「所定之編號」。行政機關藐視本院，逾越本法授權，自訂解釋，致扭曲本法涵義，殊不可取。茲明定許可字號為經行政機關審核准用之許可證字號。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康中黑體">委員劉建國等<span lang="EN-US">22</span>人提案：</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">將本條第三款後段之「許可字號」修正為「許可證字號」，更明確定義為「許可證字號」，以防止衍生其他誤導性解釋。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康中黑體">委員田秋堇等<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人所提修正動議：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第三條　本法用詞，定義如下：</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、食品：指以適於人食用之農林漁牧產品或原料，生鮮或加工供人飲食、咀嚼或以其他方式攝入體內之可食用物質，但嗜好性之菸、酒及檳榔除外。食品不應包括飼料、殘留物及污染物。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">二、特殊營養食品：指嬰兒與較大嬰兒配方食品、特定疾病配方食品及其他經中央主管機關許可得供特殊營養需求者使用之配方食品。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">三、食品添加物：指為食品著色、調味、防腐、漂白、乳化、增加香味、安定品質、促進發酵、增加稠度、強化營養、防止氧化或其他必要目的，加入、接觸於食品之單方或複方物質。複方食品添加物使用之添加物僅限由中央主管機關准用之食品添加物組成，前述准用之單方食品添加物皆應有中央主管機關之審核准用許可證字號。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">四、食品器具：指與食品或食品添加物直接接觸之器械、工具或器皿。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">五、食品容器或包裝：指與食品或食品添加物直接接觸之容器或包裹物。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">六、食品用洗潔劑：指用於消毒或洗滌食品、食品器具、食品容器或包裝之物質。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">七、食品業者：指從事食品或食品添加物之製造、加工、調配、包裝、運送、貯存、販賣、輸入、輸出或從事食品器具、食品容器或包裝、食品用洗潔劑之製造、加工、輸入、輸出或販賣之業者。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">八、標示：指於食品、食品添加物、食品用洗潔劑、食品器具、食品容器或包裝上，記載品名或為說明之文字、圖畫、記號或附加之說明書。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">九、營養標示：指於食品容器或包裝上，記載食品之營養成分、含量及營養宣稱。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">十、查驗：指查核及檢驗。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">十一、基因改造：指使用基因工程或分子生物技術，將遺傳物質轉移或轉殖入活細胞或生物體，產生基因重組現象，使表現具外源基因特性或使自身特定基因無法表現之相關技術。但不包括傳統育種、同科物種之細胞及原生質體融合、雜交、誘變、體外受精、體細胞變異及染色體倍增等技術。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康中黑體">審查會：</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第三條條文：委員田秋堇等</span><span lang="EN-US">26</span><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:
  &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">人、委員劉建國等</span><span lang="EN-US">22</span><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">人提案及委員田秋堇等</span><span lang="EN-US">3</span><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">人所提修正動議均保留。</span></p>
  </td>

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:

  <td width="270" valign="top" style="width:134.9pt;border-top:none;border-left:

  mso-border-alt:solid windowtext .5pt;padding:1.4pt 1.4pt 1.4pt 1.4pt">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
  </td>
  <td width="270" valign="top" style="width:134.95pt;border-top:none;border-left:
  none;border-bottom:solid windowtext 1.0pt;border-right:solid windowtext 1.0pt;
  mso-border-top-alt:solid windowtext .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid windowtext .5pt;
  mso-border-alt:solid windowtext .5pt;padding:1.4pt 1.4pt 1.4pt 1.4pt">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康中黑體">委員陳亭妃等<span lang="EN-US">21</span>人提案：</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第四條　主管機關採行之食品安全管理措施應以風險評估為基礎，符合滿足國民享有之健康、安全食品以及知的權利、科學證據原則、<u>無預警稽查與</u>事先預防原則、資訊透明原則，建構風險評估以及諮議體系。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">前項風險評估，中央主管機關應召集食品安全、毒理與風險評估等專家學者及民間團體組成食品風險評估諮議會為之。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第一項諮議體系應就食品衛生安全與營養、基因改造食品、食品廣告標示、食品檢驗方法等成立諮議會，召集食品安全、營養學、醫學、毒理、風險管理、農業、法律、人文社會領域相關具有專精學者組成之。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">諮議會之組成、議事、程序與範圍及其他應遵行事項之辦法，由中央主管機關定之。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">中央主管機關對重大或突發性食品衛生安全事件<u>應依</u>風險評估或流行病學調查結果，公告對特定產品或特定地區之產品採取下列管理措施：</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、限制或停止輸入查驗、製造及加工之方式或條件。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">二、下架、封存、限期回收、限期改製、沒入銷毀。</span></p>

  <td width="270" valign="top" style="width:134.95pt;border-top:none;border-left:

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第四條　主管機關採行之食品安全管理措施應以風險評估為基礎，符合滿足國民享有之健康、安全食品以及知的權利、科學證據原則、事先預防原則、資訊透明原則，建構風險評估以及諮議體系。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">前項風險評估，中央主管機關應召集食品安全、毒理與風險評估等專家學者及民間團體組成食品風險評估諮議會為之。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第一項諮議體系應就食品衛生安全與營養、基因改造食品、食品廣告標示、食品檢驗方法等成立諮議會，召集食品安全、營養學、醫學、毒理、風險管理、農業、法律、人文社會領域相關具有專精學者組成之。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康中黑體">委員陳亭妃等<span lang="EN-US">21</span>人提案：</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、近年來食品安全的漏洞頻出，從三聚氰胺、塑化劑、瘦肉精、毒澱粉與假油，到今年爆發強冠公司製作餿水油、黑心豬油流竄全台與外銷他國，對此，國人不禁要問的是，為何在經歷衛生署組織升格為衛生福利部（食品藥物管理局提升為食品藥物管理署）及食品衛生管理法於去年（</span><span lang="EN-US">2013</span><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:
  &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">年）</span><span lang="EN-US">6</span><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">月新修訂後，卻仍有如此大規模的違法事件，政府的食安防線到底在那裡？是以，建立一套主動式食安預防機制方為長久之道。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">二、其次，廠商自負產品安全的責任乃天經地義，也是世界潮流。但是，即使在人力經費短缺之下，政府不可完全倚賴廠商自主管理，主管機關仍須「強化無預警稽查」，包括樣本檢驗，以及追查原料來源等，尤其是針對影響層面可能較大的廠商加以優先稽查，以達嚇阻之效。</span></p>

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">諮議會之組成、議事、程序與範圍及其他應遵行事項之辦法，由中央主管機關定之。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">中央主管機關對重　大或突發性食品衛生安全事件，必要時得依風險評估或流行病學調查結果，公告對特定產品或特定地區之產品採取下列管理措施：</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、限制或停止輸入查驗、製造及加工之方式或條件。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">二、下架、封存、限期回收、限期改製、沒入銷毀。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康中黑體">審查會：</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第四條條文：委員陳亭妃等</span><span lang="EN-US">21</span><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:
  &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">人提案及委員田秋堇等</span><span lang="EN-US">3</span><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">人、委員陳節如等</span><span lang="EN-US">3</span><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">人所提修正動議均保留。</span></p>

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:

 <tr style="mso-yfti-irow:6">
  <td width="270" valign="top" style="width:134.9pt;border:solid windowtext 1.0pt;
  border-top:none;mso-border-top-alt:solid windowtext .5pt;mso-border-alt:solid windowtext .5pt;
  padding:1.4pt 1.4pt 1.4pt 1.4pt">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">（修正通過）</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第七條　食品業者應實施自主管理，訂定食品安全監測計畫，確保食品衛生安全。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">食品業者應將其產品原材料、半成品或成品，自行或送交其他檢驗機關（構）、法人或團體檢驗。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">上市、上櫃及其他經中央主管機關公告類別及規模之食品業者，應設置實驗室，從事前項自主檢驗。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第一項應訂定食品安全監測計畫之食品業者類別與規模，與第二項應辦理檢驗之食品業者類別與規模、最低檢驗週期，及其他相關事項，由中央主管機關公告。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">食品業者於發現產品有危害衛生安全之虞時，應即主動停止製造、加工、販賣及辦理回收，並通報直轄市、縣（市）主管機關。</span></p>
  </td>
  <td width="270" valign="top" style="width:134.9pt;border-top:none;border-left:
  none;border-bottom:solid windowtext 1.0pt;border-right:solid windowtext 1.0pt;
  mso-border-top-alt:solid windowtext .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid windowtext .5pt;
  mso-border-alt:solid windowtext .5pt;padding:1.4pt 1.4pt 1.4pt 1.4pt">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;

  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康中黑體">委員江惠貞等<span lang="EN-US">18</span>人提案：</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、本法所稱之「食品業者」所指乃指「從事食品或食品添加物之製造、加工、調配、包裝、運送、貯存、販賣、輸入、輸出或從事食品器具、食品容器或包裝、食品用洗潔劑之製造、加工、輸入、輸出或販賣之業者。」從食品原料、製造，至後端配送、販賣均包含在內，範圍甚廣。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">二、目前法規雖能落實食品業者自主管理，然考量對食品安全影響最大者，乃實際從事食品製造、加工、調配、輸入之業者，為免重複檢驗，浪費社會資源，此項檢驗責任應明訂由能實際影響食品成分之業者負擔。故第二項新增製造、加工調配、輸入食品業者就所生產販售之產品材料、半成品或成品，應予以檢驗。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">三、第三項新增。負責食品販賣之業者，如各大通路商與大型連鎖商已針對所販售商品收取高額上架費，實不應對上架販售的食品成分內容毫無所悉，待爆發食安事件時則以僅負責販售為由推卸責任。雖不用再重複施行檢驗，但仍須規範販賣食品之業者要求上架產品檢附檢驗報告，以達為所販賣之食品做初步把關之目的，同時負起販售良心商品的責任，否則商人僅以販售商品獲利為目標，對商品品質如何卻無任何責任，犧牲的永遠只是消費者的食安權益。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">四、因應新增第三項，本項次序遞移。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康中黑體">委員呂玉玲等<span lang="EN-US">19</span>人提案：</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、本條修正。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">二、無論是否為食品業者自行設立或其他檢驗機關（構）、法人或團體之檢驗單位，都應該是經中央主管機關認證之檢驗單位，同時為確實食品安全衛生把關，建議應經技師簽證，以昭公信。又為與食品業者依第八條第二項所公告之食品安全管制系統準則所僱用之全職食品技師做區隔，應必須明確規定其所僱用之專職食品技師不得執行簽證。爰修正第三項與第四項。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康中黑體">委員陳亭妃等<span lang="EN-US">21</span>人提案：</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、食品安全的漏洞頻出，對此，國人不禁要問的是，政府的食安防線到底在那裡？為何政府的檢驗，測不出問題油品的缺失？其實食品的檢驗與查核是需要配套，是以，建立一套主動式食安預防機制方為長久之道。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">二、自主管理需有各級主管機關「主動式稽查」之配套：政府不可完全倚賴廠商自主管理，主管機關應配合主動式稽查檢驗。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">三、其次，直轄市、縣（市）主管機關一旦發現食品業者之產品有危害衛生安全時，應立即要求業者停止製造、加工、販賣等，以加強打擊查緝地下工廠，避免其不法行徑，也能保護合法廠商之權益，確保食品衛生安全。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康中黑體">委員劉建國等<span lang="EN-US">22</span>人提案：</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">鑒於幾次食安風暴，關於「業者自主管理制度」成效不彰，現行尚無食品業者實施自主管理之「全面性」規範，僅要求業者注意食品品質並不足夠，除應由中央主管機關加強業者自主管理機制並納入罰則外，業者並應自主揭露正確資料，以確保消費者食品衛生安全。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康中黑體">審查會：</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第七條條文修正通過，修正為：「食品業者應實施自主管理，訂定食品安全監測計畫，確保食品衛生安全。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">食品業者應將其產品原材料、半成品或成品，自行或送交其他檢驗機關（構）、法人或團體檢驗。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">上市、上櫃及其他經中央主管機關公告類別及規模之食品業者，應設置實驗室，從事前項自主檢驗。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第一項應訂定食品安全監測計畫之食品業者類別與規模，與第二項應辦理檢驗之食品業者類別與規模、最低檢驗週期，及其他相關事項，由中央主管機關公告。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">食品業者於發現產品有危害衛生安全之虞時，應即主動停止製造、加工、販賣及辦理回收，並通報直轄市、縣（市）主管機關。」</span></p>
  </td>

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:

  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康中黑體">委員呂玉玲等<span lang="EN-US">19</span>人提案：</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第八條之一　中央主管機關應依第三條第七款食品業者之安全衛生、風險與經營記錄等情形，以分期分類整批或個別方式，公告其相關食品應經食品技師簽證。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">前項技師得聘請技士協助辦理簽證以外之業務。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:

  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">中央主管機關應建置食品安全衛生管理資訊網路平臺，供民眾查詢並蒐集資訊，其辦法由中央主管機關定之。</span></p>

  <td width="270" valign="top" style="width:134.95pt;border-top:none;border-left:
  none;border-bottom:solid windowtext 1.0pt;border-right:solid windowtext 1.0pt;
  mso-border-top-alt:solid windowtext .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid windowtext .5pt;
  mso-border-alt:solid windowtext .5pt;padding:1.4pt 1.4pt 1.4pt 1.4pt">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康中黑體">委員呂玉玲等<span lang="EN-US">19</span>人提案：</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、本條新增。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">二、為與中央主管機關依第八條所公告之食品安全管制系統由食品業者所自聘之食品技師做區別，爰稱簽證技師為外部食品技師，同時因為考慮政府現有人力及初期技師人力不足因素，故建議技師得聘請技士（不得獨立執業）協助辦理簽證以外之業務，故建議中央主管機關亦應對簽證技師與技士之資格、執業、業務、簽證項目、服務家數與收費之限制、責任、訓練、處罰、獎勵、登錄全國食品安全衛生管理資訊系統及其他應遵守事項訂定管理辦法。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">三、鑒於食品業的複雜性、多元性與獲利性不同，中央主管機關可依其安全衛生、風險性質或業者之經營記錄等情形，將其分期分類（如上、中、下游、原料提供、製造、通路、販賣、躉售、零售、餐廳、傳統市集、臨時性或短暫性的市集、營業額或規模），視實際需要以整批或個別方式公告其相關食品產物應經外部食品技師簽證。但對於應支付給食品技師（士）一定的服務費用，由於將來其服務之對象會增多，中央主管機關應該對其服務收費與服務家數做合理規範，並可依實際情形時做調整，一來係為避免惡性競爭的現象，二來能讓食品業者享有良好的諮詢輔導服務，又免因負擔過重繼而將此列為成本轉價給消費者。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">四、為期發揮食品技師協助主管機關輔導食品業者之最大管理功能，中央主管機關應訂定相關管理辦法，規定技師對於所輔導食品業者之相關簽證資訊登錄於全國食品安全衛生管理資訊系統。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">五、為與全國食品安全衛生管理資訊系統做適當結合，公開相關資訊以供民眾查詢並蒐集資訊，授權中央主管機關應建置網路平臺並管理之。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康中黑體">審查會：</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第八條之一條文：委員呂玉玲等</span><span lang="EN-US">19</span><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:
  &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">人提案不予增訂。</span></p>

  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、本條修正。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">二、配合第八條之一之新增，建議亦應經食品技師簽證，以求落實。爰修正第一項。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">三、由於食品安全衛生涉及之範疇繁多，並橫跨多個相關部會，建議應建立法源依據，授權食品安全衛生中央主管機關會同相關部會訂定相關辦法為之。爰修正第二項。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康中黑體">委員田秋堇等<span lang="EN-US">26</span>人提案：</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、新增第二項條文，原第二項順延為第三項。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">二、主管機關雖要求食品業者自行建立追溯追蹤系統及業者登錄制度，然此兩項措施均賴業者主動建立及登錄，資料之正確與否有賴主管機關到場稽查，稽查難度大且將耗費大量人力，主管機關應與財政部協商，將交易發票列入連線登錄，發票內容應包括品名及數量，以利查核登錄之真實性，落實源頭管理之目的。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康中黑體">審查會：</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第九條條文修正通過，修正為：「經中央主管機關公告類別與規模之食品業者，應依其產業模式，建立產品原材料、半成品與成品供應來源及流向之追溯或追蹤系統。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">中央主管機關為管理食品安全衛生及品質，確保食品追溯或追蹤系統資料之正確性，應就前項之業者，依溯源之必要性，分階段公告使用電子發票。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">中央主管機關應建立第一項之追溯或追蹤系統，食品業者應以電子方式申報追溯或追蹤系統之資料，其電子申報方式及規格由中央主管機關定之。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
