  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康中黑體">民進黨黨團提案：</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">近幾次食安事件均源於非食品級原料流入並混充於食品中，目前國內部分廠商同時具有食品與飼料廠之執照，國內外非食用原物料、添加物混充流入食品供應鏈管理不易。爰增列第三項，要求從事食品或食品添加物之食品工廠應單獨設立，採取「分廠分照」制度，也就是食品廠只有做食品的執照，不得同時從事非食品的製造、加工、調配。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康中黑體">委員林淑芬等<span lang="EN-US">17</span>人提案：</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">我國食品工廠多同時具有食品製造、化學材料製造業、飼料廠等工廠登記證造成非食品級、食品原料混充，以致管理不易，滋生弊端。為落實食品安全、杜絕非食品級原料混充於食品內，爰提案要求食品工廠應單獨設立，落實「分廠分照」制度。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康中黑體">審查會：</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第十條條文修正通過，修正為：「食品業者之設廠登記，應由工業主管機關會同主管機關辦理。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">食品工廠之建築及設備，應符合設廠標準；其標準，由中央主管機關會同中央工業主管機關定之。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">從事食品或食品添加物製造之工廠應單獨設立，不得於同一廠址及廠房同時從事非食品之製造、加工、調配。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">本法中華民國○年○月○日修正施行前，前項之工廠未單獨設立者，由中央主管機關分階段公告，並應於公告後一年內完成辦理。」</span></p>
  </td>

  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:

  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、修訂本條文第二項。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:

  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">二、針對日前大統公司油品造假，許多消費者紛紛退貨求償，詢問能否據以求償？惟該公司產品雖表示有投保產品責任險</span><span lang="EN-US">1,000</span><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:
  &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">萬元，但是產險業者同業皆稱不知大統是由哪家承保，懷疑可能連該公司產品責任險也是「虛晃一招」，沒有實際投保，而就算有投保</span><span lang="EN-US">1,000</span><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:
  &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">萬元，也與其營運規模不成比例。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">三、顯見，政府對於廠商強制投保責任險的執行力不足，致使少數不肖業者投保產品責任險額度與其營運規模不成比例、甚至造假，導致保障消費者之生命權有限，民眾「食的安全」顯然不受保障，加上，產險公會亦曾表示，我國產品責任險制度有很大補強空間。又，近年來消費者權益意識抬頭，為保障其權益、降低食品危害之疑慮，以及健全整體食品安全環境，應依照業者之營運規模等比例投保產品責任保險，並於明顯處標示保險金額。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:

  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:

  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">八、逾有效日期。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:

  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">前項第五款、第六款殘留農藥或動物用藥安全容許量及食品中原子塵或放射能污染安全容許量之標準，由中央主管機關會商相關機關定之。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;

  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第一項第三款有害人體健康之物質，包括雖非疫區而近十年內有發生牛海綿狀腦病或新型庫賈氏症病例之國家或地區牛隻之頭骨、腦、眼睛、脊髓、絞肉、內臟及其他相關產製品。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:

  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">國內外之肉品及其他相關產製品，除依中央主管機關根據國人膳食習慣為風險評估所訂定安全容許標準者外，不得檢出乙型受體素。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:

  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">七、攙偽或假冒。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">八、從未於國內供作飲食且未經證明為無害人體健康。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">九、添加未經中央主管機關許可之添加物。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">前項第五款、第六款殘留農藥或動物用藥安全容許量及食品中原子塵或放射能污染安全容許量之標準，由中央主管機關會商相關機關定之。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第一項第三款有害人體健康之物質，包括雖非疫區而近十年內有發生牛海綿狀腦病或新型庫賈氏症病例之國家或地區牛隻之頭骨、腦、眼睛、脊髓、絞肉、內臟及其他相關產製品。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">國內外之肉品及其他相關產製品，除依中央主管機關根據國人膳食習慣為風險評估所訂定安全容許標準者外，不得檢出乙型受體素。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">國內外如發生因食用安全容許殘留乙型受體素肉品導致中毒案例時，應立即停止含乙型受體素之肉品進口；國內經確認有因食用致中毒之個案，政府應負照護責任，並協助向廠商請求損害賠償。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康中黑體">委員葉津鈴等<span lang="EN-US">16</span>人提案：</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第十五條　食品或食品添加物有下列情形之一者，不得製造、加工、調配、包裝、運送、貯存、販賣、輸入、輸出、作為贈品或公開陳列：</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、變質或腐敗。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">二、未成熟而有害人體健康。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">三、有毒或含有害人體健康之物質或異物。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">四、染有病原性生物，或經流行病學調查認定屬造成食品中毒之病因。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">五、殘留農藥或動物用藥含量超過安全容許量。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">六、受原子塵或放射能污染，其含量超過安全容許量。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">七、攙偽或假冒。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">八、逾有效日期。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">九、從未於國內供作飲食且未經證明為無害人體健康。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">十、添加未經中央主管機關許可之添加物。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><u><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">十一、不宜供人食用。</span></u></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">前項第五款、第六款殘留農藥或動物用藥安全容許量及食品中原子塵或放射能污染安全容許量之標準，由中央主管機關會商相關機關定之。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第一項第三款有害人體健康之物質，包括雖非疫區而近十年內有發生牛海綿狀腦病或新型庫賈氏症病例之國家或地區牛隻之頭骨、腦、眼睛、脊髓、絞肉、內臟及其他相關產製品。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:

  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第十五條　食品或食品添加物有下列情形之一者，不得製造、加工、調配、包裝、運送、貯存、販賣、輸入、輸出、作為贈品或公開陳列：</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:

  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:

  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">二、未成熟而有害人體健康。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">三、有毒或含有害人體健康之物質或異物。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:

  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">六、受原子塵或放射能污染，其含量超過安全容許量。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">七、攙偽或假冒。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">八、逾有效日期。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">九、從未於國內供作飲食且未經證明為無害人體健康。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">十、添加未經中央主管機關許可之添加物。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">前項第五款、第六款殘留農藥或動物用藥安全容許量及食品中原子塵或放射能污染安全容許量之標準，由中央主管機關會商相關機關定之。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第一項第三款有害人體健康之物質，包括雖非疫區而近十年內有發生牛海綿狀腦病或新型庫賈氏症病例之國家或地區牛隻之頭骨、腦、眼睛、脊髓、絞肉、內臟及其他相關產製品。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">國內外之肉品及其他相關產製品，除依中央主管機關根據國人膳食習慣為風險評估所訂定安全容許標準者外，不得檢出乙型受體素。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">國內外如發生因食用安全容許殘留乙型受體素肉品導致中毒案例時，應立即停止含乙型受體素之肉品進口；國內經確認有因食用致中毒之個案，政府應負照護責任，並協助向廠商請求損害賠償。</span></p>
  </td>
  <td width="270" valign="top" style="width:134.95pt;border-top:none;border-left:
  none;border-bottom:solid windowtext 1.0pt;border-right:solid windowtext 1.0pt;
  mso-border-top-alt:solid windowtext .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid windowtext .5pt;
  mso-border-alt:solid windowtext .5pt;padding:1.4pt 1.4pt 1.4pt 1.4pt">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康中黑體">委員孫大千等<span lang="EN-US">22</span>人提案：</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、本款新增。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">二、食用色素增加食品顏色，不僅能提升食用者食慾，同時增添感官享受，在普遍追求食品色香味俱全的台灣，便被積極添加入食品中。然，由於天然色素供應不足且價格較為高昂，市面上舉凡糖果、蛋糕等食品，其添加在食品內之色素多為人工色素。據國內外多項研究指出，除一般人食用人工色素可能造成肝腎功能受損、食慾不振外，對於嬰幼兒更可能造成生長遲緩、引發嚴重過敏反應、增加罹患過動症及注意力不集中之風險。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">三、爰提案增訂「食品安全衛生管理法」第十五條第一項第十一款，明文規定嬰幼兒食品中添加之食用色素不得使用任何人工色素，以維護兒童之健康成長。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康中黑體">委員李慶華等<span lang="EN-US">16</span>人提案：</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">配合第四十四條第一項第二款修正及擴大第四十九條第一項處罰範圍，爰刪除第一項第八款。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康中黑體">委員葉津鈴等<span lang="EN-US">16</span>人提案：</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">香港立法例，《公眾衛生及市政條例》（第</span><span lang="EN-US">132</span><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:
  &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">章）第</span><span lang="EN-US">54</span><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">條規定，凡出售不宜供人食用的食物，即屬犯罪。因此，增列第一項十一款不宜供人食用。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康中黑體">委員吳育仁等<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人所提修正動議：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">食品安全衛生管理法第十五條中第一項三款「有毒或含有害人體健康之物質或異物」中，文字修正為「不適合供人體食用之食品」，以避免黑心廠商因為受害民眾不易舉證之故，而輕易逃脫法律之制裁。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康中黑體">委員林淑芬等<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人所提修正動議：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第十五條第一項第六款修正如下「六、受原子塵或放射能污染。」</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康中黑體">審查會：</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第十五條條文：委員孫大千等</span><span lang="EN-US">22</span><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:
  &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">人、委員李慶華等</span><span lang="EN-US">16</span><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">人、委員葉津鈴等</span><span lang="EN-US">16</span><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:
  &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">人提案及委員吳育仁等</span><span lang="EN-US">5</span><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">人、委員林淑芬等</span><span lang="EN-US">3</span><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">人所提修正動議均保留。</span></p>

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:

  </td>
  <td width="270" valign="top" style="width:134.95pt;border-top:none;border-left:
  none;border-bottom:solid windowtext 1.0pt;border-right:solid windowtext 1.0pt;
  mso-border-top-alt:solid windowtext .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid windowtext .5pt;
  mso-border-alt:solid windowtext .5pt;padding:1.4pt 1.4pt 1.4pt 1.4pt">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康中黑體">委員蔣乃辛等<span lang="EN-US">17</span>人提案：</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第二十二條　食品之容器或外包裝，應以中文及通用符號，明顯標示下列事項：</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、品名。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">二、內容物名稱；其為二種以上混合物時，應依其含量多寡由高至低分別標示之。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:

  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:

  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">部分廠商常將其販售或推銷的食品在電視、平面媒體、網路或超商預購中大打「名廚、名人」廣告吸客，但這些食品實際上並非名廚或名人親自監製，僅是借其知名度代言廣告，更甚者是找其他廠商代工或監製，並非販售公司設廠製造，但這些薦證廣告卻導致消費者誤解購買與權益的受損。為維護消費者的權益，與產品資訊的透明度，本席等爰增列第一項第十款，明訂商品或服務之薦證者、代工廠商或監製廠商之委託（任）、監製或薦證等相關資訊，應於商品或服務之包裝或廣告中加大字體明確標示與說明；原第十款，依序改為第十一款。</span></p>

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:

 <tr style="mso-yfti-irow:15">
  <td width="270" valign="top" style="width:134.9pt;border:solid windowtext 1.0pt;
  border-top:none;mso-border-top-alt:solid windowtext .5pt;mso-border-alt:solid windowtext .5pt;
  padding:1.4pt 1.4pt 1.4pt 1.4pt">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">（修正通過）</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第三十二條　主管機關為追查或預防食品衛生安全事件，必要時得要求食品業者、非食品業者或其代理人提供輸入產品之相關紀錄、文件及電子檔案或資料庫，食品業者、非食品業者或其代理人不得規避、妨礙或拒絕。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">食品業者應就前項輸入產品、基因改造食品原料之相關紀錄、文件及電子檔案或資料庫保存五年。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:

  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;

  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康中黑體">審查會：</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:

  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康中黑體">委員呂玉玲等<span lang="EN-US">19</span>人提案：</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第三十七條　食品、食品添加物、食品器具、食品容器或包裝及食品用洗潔劑之檢驗<u>，以下列方式辦理：</u></span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><u><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、經認證之相關機關（構）、法人或團體。</span></u></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><u><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">二、各級主管機關所屬食品衛生檢驗機構。其得將檢驗之一部或全部，委任、委託前款單位辦理。</span></u></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">中央主管機關<u>應</u>就前項受委任、委託之相關機關（構）、法人或團體，辦理認證；必要時，其認證工作，得委任、委託相關機關（構）、法人或團體辦理。<u>但被認證者與認證者，不得為同一人、有關係企業或隸屬關係。</u></span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">前二項有關檢驗之委託、檢驗機關（構）、法人或團體認證之條件與程序、委託辦理認證工作之程序及其他相關事項之管理辦法，由中央主管機關定之。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><u><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第一項經認證之相關機關（構）、法人或團體之職責、獎勵、處罰、檢驗費用、檢驗技術之提升與其他相關事項之管理辦法，由中央主管機關定之。</span></u></p>
  </td>
  <td width="270" valign="top" style="width:134.95pt;border-top:none;border-left:
  none;border-bottom:solid windowtext 1.0pt;border-right:solid windowtext 1.0pt;
  mso-border-top-alt:solid windowtext .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid windowtext .5pt;
  mso-border-alt:solid windowtext .5pt;padding:1.4pt 1.4pt 1.4pt 1.4pt">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第三十七條　食品、食品添加物、食品器具、食品容器或包裝及食品用洗潔劑之檢驗，由各級主管機關或委任、委託經認可之相關機關（構）、法人或團體辦理。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">中央主管機關得就前項受委任、委託之相關機關（構）、法人或團體，辦理認證；必要時，其認證工作，得委任、委託相關機關（構）、法人或團體辦理。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">前二項有關檢驗之委託、檢驗機關（構）、法人或團體認證之條件與程序、委託辦理認證工作之程序及其他相關事項之管理辦法，由中央主管機關定之。</span></p>
  </td>
  <td width="270" valign="top" style="width:134.95pt;border-top:none;border-left:
  none;border-bottom:solid windowtext 1.0pt;border-right:solid windowtext 1.0pt;
  mso-border-top-alt:solid windowtext .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid windowtext .5pt;
  mso-border-alt:solid windowtext .5pt;padding:1.4pt 1.4pt 1.4pt 1.4pt">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康中黑體">委員呂玉玲等<span lang="EN-US">19</span>人提案：</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、本條修正。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">二、為配合第八條之一新增條文中有關食品技師（士）與檢驗機構之增列，建議未來檢驗工作應可分由外部獨立食品技師送至相關經認證之檢驗機關（構）、法人或團體，或由其所聘用之食品技師送至所服務經認證之檢驗機關（構）、法人或團體為之。同時考量各級主管機關所屬食品衛生檢驗機構之預算、人力、檢驗數量之負荷能力與技術等問題，建議可視實際情況將其檢驗之一部或全部，委任、委託經認證之機關（構）、法人或團體辦理。爰修正第一項。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">三、由於第一項之相關機關（構）、法人或團體是指應經認證通過者方有資格辦理，故第二項中央主管機關對於認證之辦理是屬一定要做的工作，故將「得」修正為「應」。同時被認證者與認證者，不得為同一人、有關係企業或隸屬關係。爰修正第二項。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">四、對於經認證之相關機關（構）、法人或團體之職責、獎勵、處罰與鼓勵其對檢驗技術之提升發展，建議授權由中央主管機關訂定辦法管理。此外，由於將來送檢驗機構檢驗之對象會增多，故對檢驗收費做合理規範，並可依實際情形時做調整，一來為避免惡性競爭，二來能讓食品業者免因負擔過重繼而將此列為成本轉價給消費者。惟在實施過程中對於收入較不豐碩或無規模可言的業者（如攤販），如將來有在公告實施對象之列，其應支付給檢驗機構之檢驗費用如果有困難之處，主管機關應要給予必要的協助，或者此部分之檢驗就由主管機關自行負責。爰增訂第四項。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康中黑體">審查會：</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第三十七條條文：維持現行條文，不予修正。</span></p>
  </td>

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康中黑體">民進黨黨團提案：</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第四十二條之一　為維護國人享有健康安全食品並確實保障國人健康，有效遏止不良廠商之違法行為，中央政府應配置食品警察隊，協助食品衛生稽查人員，排除稽查及取締違法之阻礙，維護良好食品安全環境。</span></p>
  </td>
  <td width="270" valign="top" style="width:134.95pt;border-top:none;border-left:
  none;border-bottom:solid windowtext 1.0pt;border-right:solid windowtext 1.0pt;

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:

  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康中黑體">民進黨黨團提案：</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、本條新增。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">二、現行食品衛生稽查人員因缺乏司法強制權，現場稽查時常遇到業者不配合就碰壁，甚至稽查後被尾隨跟蹤，嚴重威脅食品衛生稽查人員人身安全。政府公權力屢遭不肖業者挑戰，民眾食不安心也嚴重影響政府威信。立法院</span><span lang="EN-US">102</span><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:
  &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">年</span><span lang="EN-US">5</span><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">月</span><span lang="EN-US">31</span><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">日三讀通過食品衛生管理法曾通過附帶決議，要求衛生署研議設立「食品警察」。然行政院卻以警力不足拒絕設立，惟食安風暴卻愈演愈烈，影響層面愈來愈大，為有效遏止不良廠商之黑心行為，爰仿照環保署民國</span><span lang="EN-US">88</span><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:
  &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">年所成立的環境保護警察隊，專責協助環保署執行環境保護相關法令，要求中央政府應配置食品警察，專責協助食品衛生稽查人員，排除稽查及取締違法之阻礙，維護良好食品安全環境。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康中黑體">委員劉建國等<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人所提修正動議：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第四十二條之一：「為維護國人享有健康安全食品並確實保障國人健康，有效遏止不良廠商之違法行為，中央政府得配置食品警察隊，排除稽查及取締違法之阻礙，維護良好食品安全環境。」</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:

  mso-border-alt:solid windowtext .5pt;padding:1.4pt 1.4pt 1.4pt 1.4pt">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第四十四條　有下列行為之一者，處新臺幣六萬元以上五千萬元以下罰鍰；情節重大者，並得命其歇業、停業一定期間、廢止其公司、商業、工廠之全部或部分登記事項，或食品業者之登錄；經廢止登錄者，一年內不得再申請重新登錄：</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、違反第八條第一項或第二項規定，經命其限期改正，屆期不改正。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">二、違反第十五條第一項、第四項或第十六條規定。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">三、經主管機關依第五十二條第二項規定，命其回收、銷毀而不遵行。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">四、違反中央主管機關依第五十四條第一項所為禁止其製造、販賣、輸入或輸出之公告。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">違反前項規定，其所得利益超過法定罰鍰最高額且經中央主管機關認定情節重大者，得於所得利益範圍內裁處之。</span></p>
  </td>
  <td width="270" valign="top" style="width:134.95pt;border-top:none;border-left:
  none;border-bottom:solid windowtext 1.0pt;border-right:solid windowtext 1.0pt;
  mso-border-top-alt:solid windowtext .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid windowtext .5pt;
  mso-border-alt:solid windowtext .5pt;padding:1.4pt 1.4pt 1.4pt 1.4pt">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康中黑體">行政院提案：</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、本法經多次修正，雖已全面加重罰則，惟仍有業者為牟取私利，以劣質原料製作食品，對民眾食品衛生安全及消費權益影響甚鉅，應予遏止。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">二、現行第四十四條及第四十九條雖定有行政罰及刑罰之規定，惟各界認為其罰則過輕，恐難以發揮遏止不法之作用，應加重處罰，以維國人健康及消費權益，爰將第一項罰鍰額度上限提高至二億元。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">三、刪除現行第二項，理由如下：</span></p>
  <p class="a" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:0cm;
  margin-left:36.9pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;mso-para-margin-right:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:
  .0001pt;text-indent:-21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:-2.0;line-height:15.75pt;
  mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:華康細明體">(</span><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:華康細明體">)</span><span style="font-family:華康細明體;
  mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">依據行政罰法第十八條規定，地方衛生機關於實務執行時，即可視違反行政法上義務行為應受責難程度、所生影響及因違反行政法上義務所得之利益，並得考量受處罰者之資力，於所得利益之範圍內酌量加重罰鍰，不受法定罰鍰最高額之限制。</span></p>
  <p class="a" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:0cm;
  margin-left:36.9pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;mso-para-margin-right:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:
  .0001pt;text-indent:-21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:-2.0;line-height:15.75pt;
  mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:華康細明體">(</span><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">二</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:華康細明體">)</span><span style="font-family:華康細明體;
  mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">本項適用於「違反前項規定且經中央主管機關認定情節重大者」，除對違反本法其他規定者，衍生法律適用疑義外，亦使地方主管機關須每案送中央主管機關認定情節是否重大，不僅與不當利得納入裁罰額度之規範目的未符，且影響行政效率及限制地方主管機關權限。</span></p>
  <p class="a" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:0cm;
  margin-left:36.9pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;mso-para-margin-right:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:
  .0001pt;text-indent:-21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:-2.0;line-height:15.75pt;
  mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:華康細明體">(</span><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">三</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:華康細明體">)</span><span style="font-family:華康細明體;
  mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">考量第一項已提高罰鍰上限及行政罰法第十八條已有規定，行政機關依上開規定裁罰時，已可立即對不法廠商予以嚴懲。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">四、考量本次修正之罰鍰額度差距大，爰配合授權中央主管機關訂定裁罰標準列為第二項，以建立執法之公平性。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康中黑體">民進黨黨團提案：</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、現行第二項雖有「追討不法利得」之設計，其要件需受限於「其所得利益超過法定罰鍰最高額」且「經中央主管機關認定情節重大者」，因此「追討不法利得」在文義解釋上被視為行政罰的一部分。且依行政罰法第</span><span lang="EN-US">26</span><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:
  &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">條第一項「刑事罰優先」的規定，此種「一罪不二罰」對食安問題係立法之大漏洞，即若業者刑事判決有罪，行政機關不能再罰鍰，必須等到無罪判決確定方可罰鍰，屆時業者恐早已脫產，則行政處罰勢將落空。因此，應明確區分本法第</span><span lang="EN-US">44</span><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:
  &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">條第一項之行政罰與第二項追討不法利得，只要不法利得逾法定罰鍰之上限者，主管機關都應追討不法利得。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">二、本法所指食品業者規模大小不一，此次修法將罰鍰上限提高，致罰鍰額度差距大，爰增列第三項，授權中央主管機關訂定裁罰標準。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康中黑體">委員王惠美等<span lang="EN-US">21</span>人提案：</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、近來爆發不肖食品業者於製造食品時，為降低成本牟取暴利，乃以劣質品混充優質品或以人工原料混充天然食材，對民眾食品衛生安全及消費者權益影響甚鉅，惟在現行法律制度上，基於「一罪不兩罰」的原則，以及現行刑法規定的最高罰金與犯罪者的獲利有可能完全不成比例，刑罰罰金往往遠遠不及不法所得，根本無法警惕業者。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">二、為提高嚇阻效果，避免危害食安事件一再發生，爰參酌現行道路交通管理處罰條例第三十五條第八項規定，增列第三項，令行政主管機關就刑事判決確定罰金不足行政罰鍰之部分命其繳納，以有效追討業者不當利得，積極維護國人健康權益。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康中黑體">委員李慶華等<span lang="EN-US">16</span>人提案：</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、有鑑於現行法令之罰鍰偏低，致使黑心廠商甘於被罰之風險製造黑心食品荼毒國人，且其販售期間累積鉅額暴利，故實有必要提高罰緩，以遏阻不肖廠商心存僥倖。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">二、為提高刑度，刪除原第一項第二款違反同法第十五條第一項者處以罰鍰之規定；並規定於同法第四十九條第一項，以增加自由刑之刑度。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">三、爰比照菸酒管理法，將現行對不肖廠商撤銷、廢止登錄，申請重新登錄時限，由一年內不得申請，提高至三年內不得申請。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康中黑體">委員鄭汝芬等<span lang="EN-US">16</span>人提案：</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">衛生福利部裁處大統公司</span><span lang="EN-US">18.5</span><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:
  &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">億之罰鍰，但因彰化地方法院判決大統公司負責人有期徒刑</span><span lang="EN-US">16</span><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">年、罰金</span><span lang="EN-US">5,000</span><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:
  &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">萬後，基於行政罰法「一罪不兩罰」與刑事罰優先的原則，衛生福利部最後撤銷大統不當利得之罰鍰。如此法例，將難以嚇阻不肖業者以身試法，爰修正食品衛生管理法第四十四條，將本法之不當利得減列刑事法律處罰後繼續執行，不受行政罰法第二十六條之限制。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康中黑體">台灣團結聯盟黨團提案：</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、為期有效遏止業者不法行為，爰將本條第一項罰則由新臺幣六萬元以上五千萬元以下罰鍰提高為臺幣十萬元以上一億元以下罰鍰。</span></p>

  <td width="270" valign="top" style="width:134.9pt;border:solid windowtext 1.0pt;

  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第四十七條　有下列行為之一者，處新臺幣三萬元以上三百萬元以下罰鍰；情節重大者，並得命其歇業、停業一定期間、廢止其公司、商業、工廠之全部或部分登記事項，或食品業者之登錄；經廢止登錄者，一年內不得再申請重新登錄：</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、違反中央主管機關依第四條所為公告。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">二、違反第七條第五項規定。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">四、違反第十一條第一項或第十二條第一項規定。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">五、違反中央主管機關依第十三條所為投保產品責任保險之規定。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">七、違反第二十一條第一項及第二項、第二十二條第一項或依第二項及第三項公告之事項、第二十四條第一項或依第二項公告之事項、第二十六條或第二十七條規定。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:

  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:

  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">十、規避、妨礙或拒絕本法所規定之查核、檢驗、查扣或封存。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:

  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">十一、對依本法規定應提供之資料，拒不提供或提供資料不實。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:

  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康中黑體">委員田秋堇等<span lang="EN-US">26</span>人提案：</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:

  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">七、違反第二十一條第一項及第二項、第二十二條第一項或依第二項及第三項公告之事項、第二十四條第一項或依第二項公告之事項、第二十六條或第二十七條規定。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">八、除第四十八條第七款規定者外，違反中央主管機關依第十八條所定標準中有關食品添加物規格及其使用範圍、限量之規定。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:

  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">十、規避、妨礙或拒絕本法所規定之查核、檢驗、查扣或封存。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">十一、對依本法規定應提供之資料，拒不提供或提供資料不實。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:

  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">四、違反中央主管機關依第十七條或第十九條所定標準之規定。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">五、食品業者販賣之產品違反中央主管機關依第十八條所定食品添加物規格及其使用範圍、限量之規定。</span></p>

  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康中黑體">審查會：</span></p>

  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
