  <td width="270" valign="top" style="width:134.95pt;border-top:none;border-left:
  none;border-bottom:solid windowtext 1.0pt;border-right:solid windowtext 1.0pt;
  mso-border-top-alt:solid windowtext .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid windowtext .5pt;
  mso-border-alt:solid windowtext .5pt;padding:1.4pt 1.4pt 1.4pt 1.4pt">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康中黑體">行政院提案：</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、本法雖定有相關刑罰規定，然仍無法有效遏止不肖業者之不法行為，部分食品業者仍有攙偽、假冒等不法行為，爰提高第一項至第四項之刑度及罰金，並刪除現行第一項及第二項得處拘役或選科罰金刑之規定，避免違法者之僥倖心態，以為嚇阻。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">二、惟因違規食品態樣眾多，食品業者規模大小亦有差異，考量法律衡平性，對情節輕微者，以維持現行刑度為宜，以符合罪刑相當原則，爰增列第一項後段文字。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">三、鑒於一行為同時觸犯刑事法律及違反行政法上義務規定，依行政罰法第二十六條第一項規定，依刑事法律處罰之，爰衛生主管機關對於法人欲處以行政罰鍰者，將因第五項之規定而受限，且考量違反本法相關規定之行政罰鍰已全面加重，為有效迅速嚴懲不法廠商，爰刪除第五項罰金刑之規定。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康中黑體">民進黨黨團提案：</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、近幾年食安問題年年發生，本法雖已修法多次，卻仍然無法有效遏止不肖業者之不法行為，爰提高第一項至第四項之刑度及罰金。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">二、本法所指食品業者規模大小不一，考量罪刑相當原則，情節輕微者，以維持現行刑度為宜，爰增列第一項後段文字。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康中黑體">委員劉建國等<span lang="EN-US">22</span>人提案：</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">鑒於</span><span lang="EN-US">2013</span><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:
  &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">年</span><span lang="EN-US">5</span><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">月「毒澱粉」事件，不肖廠商使用未經核准之順丁烯二酸酐（</span><span lang="EN-US">Maleicanhydride</span><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:
  &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">，又名馬來酸酐，分子式為</span><span lang="EN-US">C4H2O 3</span><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">）化製澱粉等添加物於常用食品，由於順丁烯二酸酐屬化學工業原料，主要作為聚酯樹脂、醇酸塗覆樹脂、殺蟲劑等工業用途使用，其外包裝有黏貼危險標誌，且順丁烯二酸酐為有害人體健康及從未於國內供作飲食且未經證明為無害人體健康之妨害衛生物質，不得添加至食品中，危害消費者身體健康甚鉅，爰於本條第一項新增第十五條第三款「有毒或含有害人體健康之物質或異物」及第九款「從未於國內供作飲食且未經證明為無害人體健康」，以嚇阻不肖業者濫用食品添加物。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;

  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">犯前項之罪，因而致人於死者，處無期徒刑或七年以上有期徒刑，得併科新臺幣二千萬元以下罰金；致重傷者，處三年以上十年以下有期徒刑，得併科新臺幣一千五百萬元以下罰金。</span></p>

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第四十九條之一　故意犯本法之罪者，因犯罪所得財物或財產上利益，除應發還被害人外，屬於犯人者，沒收之。如全部或一部不能沒收，追徵其價額或以其財產抵償。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">為保全前項財物或財產上利益之追徵或財產上之抵償，必要時，得酌量扣押其財產。</span></p>
  </td>
  <td width="270" valign="top" style="width:134.95pt;border-top:none;border-left:
  none;border-bottom:solid windowtext 1.0pt;border-right:solid windowtext 1.0pt;
  mso-border-top-alt:solid windowtext .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid windowtext .5pt;
  mso-border-alt:solid windowtext .5pt;padding:1.4pt 1.4pt 1.4pt 1.4pt">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康中黑體">行政院提案：</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、第一項文字酌作修正，使本條適用對象不限於故意犯罪者。另配合刑法規定統一法律用語，將現行「犯人」修正為「犯罪行為人」。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">二、配合修正條文第四十九條刪除第五項法人罰金刑之規定，增訂第二項定明法人因其代表人、代理人、受僱人或其他從業人員犯本法之罪而取得之財物或財產上利益應予沒收，以剝奪法人之不法利得，並使司法機關得據以扣押被告所屬公司或其雇主之財產，以避免藉由法人規避前項犯罪所得之沒收。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">三、現行第二項移列為第三項，文字酌作修正。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康中黑體">民進黨黨團提案：</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、現行適用對象僅限於故意犯罪之自然人，若被害人無法舉證行為人之故意，即無法適用沒收規定，爰將「故意」刪除，使本條適用對象不限於故意犯罪者。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">二、第一項僅規範犯罪之自然人，為擴大適用沒收範圍，爰增訂第二項將法人涵攝在沒收範圍內。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;

  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康中黑體">委員陳節如等<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人所提修正動議：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:

  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:

  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第四十九條之二　犯第四十九條之罪，於犯罪後自首，如有犯罪所得並自動繳交全部所得財物者，減輕或免除其刑；並因而查獲其他正犯或共犯者，得免除其刑。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">犯第四十九條之罪，在偵查中自白，如有犯罪所得並自動繳交全部所得財物者，減輕其刑；並因而查獲其他正犯或共犯者，得減輕其刑至二分之一。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康中黑體">委員李貴敏等<span lang="EN-US">32</span>人提案：</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第四十九條之二　食品業者因故意或過失違反本法第十五條第一項、第四項及第十六條之規定，或有第四十四條至第四十八條之行為致危害人體健康者，其所得之財產或其他利益應沒入之。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">主管機關有相當理由認受處分人為避免前項處分移轉其財產或其他利益於惡意第三人者，得追徵該第三人受移轉之財產或其他利益，或於其所受讓之財產利益範圍內，以該第三人之財產追繳或抵償。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">消費者或賠償請求權人因第一項處分而無法自受處分人受充分賠償者，得向處分機關請求發還不足額之部分。但應於處分確定之日起三十日內為之。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">前項之發還以依第一項及第二項實際收取之總額為限。不足發還者，應按比例發還之。但應扣除處分及執行之所有相關必要費用。</span></p>

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康中黑體">委員李慶華等<span lang="EN-US">16</span>人提案：</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、本條新增。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">二、新增鼓勵犯罪人自首條款，若因此查獲其他正犯或共犯，並繳交全部犯罪所得，得減免或免除其刑，以補我國食品安全查緝人員不足之問題。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">三、若犯罪人犯罪事實被查獲，但整體犯罪案情仍不明朗時，犯罪人自白並繳交全部犯罪所得，亦得以減輕其刑，以鼓勵犯罪人協助查緝犯罪事實。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康中黑體">委員李貴敏等<span lang="EN-US">32</span>人提案：</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、<u>本條新增。</u></span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">二、由於本法第四十九條之一之刑事沒收規定，我國實務見解向來認為「法人」原則上無刑事責任能力，該法條對「法人」無適用之餘地（臺灣高等法院</span><span lang="EN-US">88</span><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:
  &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">年</span><span lang="EN-US">6</span><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">月刑事法律問題研究第</span><span lang="EN-US">12</span><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:
  &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">輯第</span><span lang="EN-US">44</span><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">則研究意見意旨、臺灣高等法院台中分院</span><span lang="EN-US">101</span><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:
  &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">年度矚上易字第</span><span lang="EN-US">295</span><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">號刑事判決參照）。為有效剝奪不肖業者不法收益，杜絕其違反食品管制規範、危害國人身體健康並謀取暴利之誘因，爰增列第一項，明定業者因故意或過失違反第十五條第一項、第四項及第十六條之規定，或因故意有第四十四條至第四十八條之行為致危害他人健康者，其所得之財產或其他利益，均為行政處分沒入之客體。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">三、為避免不肖業者脫產致剝奪不法收益之目的不達，爰仿照美國民事沒收（</span><span lang="EN-US">civil forfeiture</span><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:
  &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">）完全剝奪牽涉不法行為之財產之宗旨，及聯邦法典第</span><span lang="EN-US">18</span><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">篇第</span><span lang="EN-US">983</span><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:
  &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">條（</span><span lang="EN-US">18 U.S .C . </span><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">§</span><span lang="EN-US">983</span><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:
  &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">）規定增訂第二項，由政府以優勢證據（</span><span lang="EN-US">preponderance of
  evidence</span><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">）證明移轉於第三人之財產或利益與不法行為間關聯，及可確認該第三人非善意不知情而應受保護之人時，得追徵其自受處分人受讓之財產或利益，或以該第三人固有之財產追繳或抵償。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">四、為保障消費者及其他受害者（如下游廠商）之權益，如沒入處分已影響其向受處分人請求賠償之權益時，本條第三項規定其得向處分機關請求發還不足之部分。且透過由國家先行沒入，其他求償人再向國家請求之制度，可兼顧相關人等因不肖業者脫產而拿不到任何賠償之不利情形，兼顧各方之公平。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">五、但為避免發還金額超過行政機關沒入、追徵、追繳或抵償而取得之金額，第四項明定發還以處分機關依第一項及第二項實際收取之總額為限，並應扣除所有行政之相關必要費用。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康中黑體">委員江惠貞等<span lang="EN-US">6</span>人所提修正動議：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第四十九條之二　因故意或過失違反本法第十五條第一項、第四項及第十六條之規定，或有第四十四條至第四十八條之行為致危害人體健康者，其所得之財產或其他利益應沒入之。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:

  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">主管機關有相當理由認受處分人為避免前項處分移轉其財產或其他利益於惡意第三人者，得追徵該第三人受移轉之財產或其他利益，或於其所受讓之財產利益範圍內，以該第三人之財產追繳或抵償。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康中黑體">委員江惠貞等<span lang="EN-US">10</span>人所提修正動議：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第四十九條之二　因故意或過失違反本法第十五條第一項、第四項及第十六條之規定；或有第四十四條至第四十八條之行為致危害人體健康者，其所得之財產或其他利益應沒入之。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">主管機關有相當理由認受處分人為避免前項處分而移轉其財產或其他利益於惡意第三人者，得沒入該第三人受移轉之財產或其他利益。如全部或一部不能沒入時，應追徵其價額或以其財產抵償之。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:

  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康中黑體">委員江惠貞等<span lang="EN-US">8</span>人所提修正動議：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;

  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第四十九條之二　經中央主管機關公告類別及規模之食品業者，因故意或過失違反本法第十五條第一項、第四項及第十六條之規定；或有第四十四條至第四十八條之行為致危害人體健康者，其所得之財產或其他利益應沒入之。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">主管機關有相當理由認受處分人為避免前項處分而移轉其財產或其他利益於惡意第三人者，得沒入該第三人受移轉之財產或其他利益。如全部或一部不能沒入者，應追徵其價額或以其財產抵償之。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第五十條　<u>食品業者</u>不得因勞工<u>合理相信食品業者有違反本法之行為，</u>向主管機關或司法機關揭露、擔任訴訟程序之證人或拒絕參與違反本法之行為而予解僱、調職或其他不利之處分。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:

  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><u><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">食品業者</span></u><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">或代表<u>食品業者</u>行使管理權之人，為前項規定所為之解僱、降調或減薪者，無效。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><u><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">前項情形，勞工以訴訟請求回復原狀，或給付因此積欠之工資或所受之財產上損害時，得請求法院令被告支付適當之律師費用、監測鑑定費用或其他訴訟費用予原告。</span></u></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><u><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">食品業者</span></u><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">以外之人曾參與違反本法規定且應負刑事責任之行為，向主管機關或司法機關揭露，因而破獲食品業者違反本法之行為者，減輕或免除其刑。</span></p>

  <td width="270" valign="top" style="width:134.95pt;border-top:none;border-left:
  none;border-bottom:solid windowtext 1.0pt;border-right:solid windowtext 1.0pt;

  mso-border-alt:solid windowtext .5pt;padding:1.4pt 1.4pt 1.4pt 1.4pt">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:

  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第五十條　雇主不得因勞工向主管機關或司法機關揭露違反本法之行為、擔任訴訟程序之證人或拒絕參與違反本法之行為而予解僱、調職或其他不利之處分。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">雇主或代表雇主行使管理權之人，為前項規定所為之解僱、降調或減薪者，無效。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">雇主以外之人曾參與違反本法之規定且應負刑事責任之行為，而向主管機關或司法機關揭露，因而破獲雇主違反本法之行為者，減輕或免除其刑。</span></p>

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:

  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、修正第一項至第三項文字，並新增第三項，原第三項順沿為第四項。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">二、美國</span><span lang="EN-US">2011</span><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:
  &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">年食品安全現代化法（</span><span lang="EN-US">Food Safety
  Modernization Act</span><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:
  &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">）在</span><span lang="EN-US">21 U.S .Code </span><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">§</span><span lang="EN-US">399d</span><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:
  &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">條文明定對吹哨者（公益通報）的種種保護措施。其中，吹哨者對於食品業者的不法行為，毋須達到能證明確有不法的程度，而只須達到客觀上合理相信有不法之程度，亦即我國司法院大法官解釋第</span><span lang="EN-US">509</span><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:
  &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">號解釋之意旨中所謂真實惡意原則即可，故於第一項加上「合理相信」以資明確。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">三、受報復之勞工通常在經濟上處於弱勢，以訴訟主張權益時若仍須負擔律師費、監測鑑定費用或其他訴訟費用，可能導致勞工放棄權益。為使勞工權益得以伸張，並懲罰進行不法報復之雇主，故增訂第三項以資週全。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康中黑體">審查會：</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第五十條條文：維持現行條文，不予修正。</span></p>

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第五十條之一　揭發者知悉食品業者違反本法之行為，得檢具事證向行政機關揭發。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:

  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康中黑體">民進黨黨團提案：</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第五十六條　（消費者之損害賠償請求權及因果關係舉證責任之分配）</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><u><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">食品業者違反本法第十五條第一項規定，致消費者之財產上損害及非財產上損害者，應負賠償責任，但有關財產上之損害賠償，能證明損害非由於其製造、加工、調配、包裝、運送、貯存、販賣、輸入、輸出所致，或於防止損害之發生已盡相當之注意者，不在此限。</span></u><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">並得準用消費者保護法第四十七條至第五十五條之規定提出消費訴訟。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如消費者不易或不能證明其實際損害額時，得請求法院依侵害情節，以每人每一事件新臺幣五百元以上三萬元以下計算。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">直轄市、縣（市）政府受理同一原因事件，致二十人以上消費者受有損害之申訴時，應協助消費者依消費者保護法第五十條之規定辦理。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康中黑體">委員田秋堇等<span lang="EN-US">26</span>人提案：</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第五十六條　<u>違反第十五條或第十六條之情形，或第二十八條第一項之標示、宣傳或廣告，有虛偽不實或引人錯誤之表示或表徵者，消費者雖無身體或健康之損害，得以購買食品之價金為財產上損害額，準用消費者保護法第四十七條至第五十五條之規定提出消費訴訟，並得請求非財產上損害賠償。</u></span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:

  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如消費者不易或不能證明<u>有損害或</u>實際損害額時，得請求法院依侵害情節，以每人每一事件新臺幣五百元以上三萬元以下計算。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">直轄市、縣（市）政府受理同一原因事件，致二十人以上消費者受有損害之申訴時，應協助消費者依消費者保護法第五十條之規定辦理。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><u><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">法院為第一項消費訴訟之判決時，得考慮不法行為之嚴重性及原告從事訴訟之公益性，依職權令被告支付適當之律師費用、監測鑑定費用或其他訴訟費用予原告。</span></u></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:

  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><u><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">受消費者保護團體委任代理消費者保護法第四十九條第一項訴訟之律師，就該訴訟得請求報酬，不受消費者保護法第四十九條第二項後段之拘束。</span></u></p>
  </td>
  <td width="270" valign="top" style="width:134.95pt;border-top:none;border-left:

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:

  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第五十六條　消費者雖非財產上之損害，亦得請求賠償相當之金額，並得準用消費者保護法第四十七條至第五十五條之規定提出消費訴訟。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如消費者不易或不能證明其實際損害額時，得請求法院依侵害情節，以每人每一事件新臺幣五百元以上三萬元以下計算。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">直轄市、縣（市）政府受理同一原因事件，致二十人以上消費者受有損害之申訴時，應協助消費者依消費者保護法第五十條之規定辦理。</span></p>
  </td>
  <td width="270" valign="top" style="width:134.95pt;border-top:none;border-left:
  none;border-bottom:solid windowtext 1.0pt;border-right:solid windowtext 1.0pt;
  mso-border-top-alt:solid windowtext .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid windowtext .5pt;
  mso-border-alt:solid windowtext .5pt;padding:1.4pt 1.4pt 1.4pt 1.4pt">
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康中黑體">民進黨黨團提案：</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、為衡平食品業者與非食品業者之商品製造人責任，爰參照民法第</span><span lang="EN-US">191</span><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:
  &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">條之</span><span lang="EN-US">1</span><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">之立法例，明文規定消費者請求權之基礎，方能有效保障消費者。倘食品業者能證明損害非由於其違法行為所致者（舉證無因果關係），或於防止損害之發生已盡相當之注意者（舉證無故意或過失），得以免責。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">二、縱使食品業者證明損害非由於其違法行為所致，或於防止損害之發生已盡相當之注意者，亦不得排除非財產上損害賠償（慰撫金）責任。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康中黑體">委員田秋堇等<span lang="EN-US">26</span>人提案：</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、修正第一項文字並新增第四項、第五項。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">二、違反第十五、十六條之情形，或第二十八條第一項所列各類產品之標示、宣傳或廣告有標示不實或引人錯誤之情形，並不一定會導致消費者健康受到損害。例如添加化學香精之麵包偽稱只含天然香精、將馬肉混入牛肉、混有人工色素而稱「天然」、「有機」的果汁、甚至在食品中添加塑化劑或餿豬油之情形，即使訴訟上舉證責任移轉，消費者也無法證明受有健康上之損害。但這些情形均屬消費者若知其情事就不會購買之詐欺行為，且此種以劣品充良品之行為構成公平交易法第二十一條第一項所指之不公平競爭行為。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">三、行政裁罰規定若行政機關怠於行使職權就形同具文。公平交易法則透過競爭者的檢舉或訴訟而啟動整頓競爭秩序的機制，但若某個產業的主要業者均採取類似的運作程序，例如</span><span lang="EN-US">GMP</span><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:
  &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">認證制度，則此種依賴競爭者啟動的機制就會失靈。考慮到食品對民眾健康的影響重要性及嚴重性，為保護消費者免受標示不實或引人錯誤宣傳方式之詐欺，而增加身體健康受損之風險，有建立此種消費詐欺訴訟類型，讓民眾循司法途徑獲得救濟之必要。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">四、消費訴訟本質上係私人之間的爭議，現行消費者保護法第四十九條第二項規定受委任律師不得請求報酬，實違反私人爭訟之法理。證券投資人及期貨交易人保護法第三十三條規定提出訴訟或仲裁之證券投資人保護機構不得請求報酬，個人資料保護法第三十九條第二項規定提出集體訴訟之法人不得請求報酬，且應委任律師代理訴訟，但均未規定律師不得請求報酬。考慮到本條消費訴訟兼具公益之性質，並為避免濫訴而有強制委任律師之必要，爰參考環境基本法第三十四條第二項，由法院依職權酌定之。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康中黑體">委員田秋堇等<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人所提修正動議：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第五十六條　（消費者之損害賠償請求權及因果關係舉證責任之轉換）</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">食品業者違反本法第十五條第一項規定時，對於消費者之財產上損害及非財產上損害應負賠償責任，並得準用消費者保護法第四十七條至第五十五條之規定提出消費訴訟。但有關財產上之損害賠償，能證明損害非由於其製造、加工、調配、包裝、運送、貯存、販賣、輸入、輸出所致，或於防止損害之發生已盡相當之注意者，不在此限。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如消費者不易或不能證明其實際損害額時，得請求法院依侵害情節，以每人每一事件新臺幣五百元以上三萬元以下計算。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">直轄市、縣（市）政府受理同一原因事件，致二十人以上消費者受有損害之申訴時，應協助消費者依消費者保護法第五十條之規定辦理。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康中黑體">委員陳節如等<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人所提修正動議：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第五十六條　違反第十五條或第十六條之情形，或第二十八條第一項之標示、宣傳或廣告，有虛偽不實或引人錯誤之表示或表徵者，消費者雖無身體或健康之損害，得以購買食品之價金為財產上之損害額，準用消費者保護法第四十七條至第五十五條之規定提出消費訴訟，並得請求非財產上損害賠償。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">違反第十五條或第十六條之情形，有致消費者健康損害之虞者，準用民法第一九五條第一項賠償消費者相當之金額。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">直轄市、縣（市）政府受理同一原因事件，致二十人以上消費者受有損害之申訴時，應協助消費者依消費者保護法第五十條之規定辦理。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">法院為第一項消費訴訟之判決時，得考慮不法行為之嚴重性及原告從事訴訟之公益性，依職權令被告支付適當之律師費用、監測鑑定費用或其他訴訟費用予原告。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">受消費者保護團體委任代理消費者保護法第四十九條第一項訴訟之律師，就該訴訟得請求報酬，不受消費者保護法第四十九條第二項後段之拘束。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康中黑體">委員江惠貞等<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人所提修正動議：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第五十六條　消費者雖非財產上之損害，亦得請求賠償相當之金額，並得準用消費者保護法第四十七條至第五十五條之規定提出消費訴訟。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如消費者不易或不能證明其實際損害額時，得請求法院依侵害情節，以每人每一事件新臺幣五百元以上三萬元以下計算。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">直轄市、縣（市）政府受理同一原因事件，致二十人以上消費者受有損害之申訴時，應協助消費者依消費者保護法第五十條之規定辦理。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">法院為第一項消費訴訟之判決時，得考慮不法行為之嚴重性及原告從事訴訟之公益性，依職權令被告支付適當之律師費用、監測鑑定費用或其他訴訟費用予原告。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;

  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">受消費者保護團體委任代理消費者保護法第四十九條第一項訴訟之律師，就該訴訟得請求報酬，不受消費者保護法第四十九條第二項後段之拘束。</span></p>

  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第五十六條之一　（食品安全保護基金之設立、來源及其用途）</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">中央主管機關為保障食品安全事件消費者之權益，得設立食品安全保護基金，並得委託其他機關（構）、法人或團體辦理。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;

  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">前項基金之來源如下：</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:

  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第二項第一款及第三款來源，以其處分生效日在中華民國一百零二年六月二十一日以後者適用。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:

  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第一項基金之用途如下：</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、補助因食品衛生安全事件依消費者保護法之規定，提起之消費訴訟相關費用。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:

  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">七、其他有關收入。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第二項第一款及第三款來源，以其處分生效日在中華民國一百零二年六月二十一日以後者適用。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:21.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第一項基金之用途如下：</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、補助因食品衛生安全事件依消費者保護法之規定，提起消費訴訟之律師報酬及訴訟相關費用。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">二、補助經公告之特定食品衛生安全事件，有關人體健康風險評估費用。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">三、補助勞工因檢舉雇主違反本法之行為，遭雇主解僱、調職或其他不利處分所提之回復原狀、給付工資及損害賠償訴訟之律師報酬及訴訟相關費用。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:26.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  1.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">四、補助其他有關促進食品安全及消費者訴訟協助相關費用。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:

  2.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:
  華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">中央主管機關應設置基金運用管理監督小組，由學者專家、消保團體、社會公正人士組成，監督補助業務。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:

  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:15.8pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-10.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:
  -1.0;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">二、現行第四十九條第五項科處法人罰金刑之規定既已刪除，則法人經依該條項判決有罪確定者，於刪除前開規定後，依刑法第二條第三項原應免予執行，然本次修正刪除前開規定，並非因其不具可罰性，而係為避免一事二罰及加速行政罰鍰之處罰，且為尊重法院原確定判決之既判力及執行力，爰增訂排除刑法第二條第三項之適用，亦即依現行第四十九條第五項規定而科處法人罰金刑之確定判決，不因刪除該項規定而免予執行。</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康中黑體">審查會：</span></p>
  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:5.25pt;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:5.25pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;
  mso-para-margin-right:.5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0cm;mso-para-margin-left:
  .5gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:15.75pt;mso-line-height-rule:
  exactly"><span style="font-family:華康細明體;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第五十九條之一條文：行政院提案保留。</span></p>
